① Consequently, discovery claims should be thought of as protoscience. ② Similar to newly staked mining claims, they are full of potential. ③ But it takes collective scrutiny and acceptance to transform a discovery claim into a mature discovery. ④ This is the credibility process, through which the individual researcher's me, here, now becomes the community's anyone, anywhere, anytime. ⑤ Objective knowledge is the goal, not the starting point.

32. It can be inferred from Paragraph 2 that credibility process requires

[A] strict inspection

[B] shared efforts.

[C] individual wisdom.

[D] persistent innovation.

##### 例24：英语二2016年Text4

① Young people who are still getting started in life were more likely than older adults to prioritize personal fulfillment in their work, to believe they will advance their careers most by regularly changing jobs, to favor communities with more public services and a faster pace of life,

to agree that couples should be financially secure before getting married or having children, and to maintain that children are best served by two parents working outside the home, the survey found.

37. It can be learned from Paragraph 3 that young people tend to _____

[A] favor a slower life pace

[B] hold an occupation longer

[C] attach importance to pre-marital finance

[D] give priority to childcare outside the home

#### 精讲

推断题跟细节题一样，都是考查对于文章细节内容的精确理解，同样可以通过静姐的“灵魂三问”法来仔细比对选项和原文，进而找到正确答案。但推断题的答案比细节题藏得更深，不像细节题的答案那样能够直接在文章中找到。推断题的难点就在于：千万不要推断！！！因为稍微一多想就容易推断过度，其实推断题的正确答案就是把文章的细节信息换一种方式表达，或归纳总结，或同义改写，或正话反说等，在稍后的例题中将详细展开说明。

推断题常见的提问形式有两种：一是跟细节题差不多，没有固定的模式；二是相对固定的提问形式，如下：

It can be inferred/learned from the text/Paragraph XXX that...

Which of the following can be inferred from Paragraph XXX about...?

注意：不需要区分细节题和推断题，因为会用到一样的解题方法，都是涉及文章的细节，都按照“灵魂三问”法比对选项和原文，只不过答案隐藏的深浅程度不同。

##### 例15: 2002年Text 3

①Yet there are good reasons to expect the economic consequences now to be less severe than in the 1970s. ②In most countries the cost of crude oil now accounts for a smaller share of the price of petrol than it did in the 1970s. ③In Europe, taxes account for up to four-fifths of  $ \underline{\text{the retail price}} $, so even quite big changes in the price of crude oil have a more muted effect on pump prices than in the past.

①然而，我们有充分的理由预计（这次油价上涨）对现在经济的影响不会像20世纪70年代那么严重。②与20世纪70年代相比，在大多数国家，现在原油成本在汽油价格中所占的份额更小。③在欧洲，税收占（汽油）零售价的比例高达五分之四，因此即使原油价格发生很大的变化，对零售价（出泵价格）的影响也比过去更小。

52 It can be inferred from the text that  $ \underline{\text{the retail price}} $ of petrol will go up dramatically if从文中可以推断出，汽油零售价格会大幅上涨，如果

题干定位

根据题干中的 the retail price（零售价格）可以定位到段3。



<table border=1 style='margin: auto; word-wrap: break-word;'><tr><td style='text-align: center; word-wrap: break-word;'>[A]</td><td style='text-align: center; word-wrap: break-word;'>price of crude oil rises. 原油价格上涨。</td><td style='text-align: center; word-wrap: break-word;'>【段3】②In most countries the cost of crude oil now accounts for a smaller share of the price of petrol than it did in the 1970s. ③In Europe, taxes account for up to four-fifths of the retail price, so even quite big changes in the price of crude oil have a more muted effect on pump prices than in the past. ②与20世纪70年代相比，在大多数国家，现在原油成本在汽油价格中所占的份额更小。③在欧洲，税收占（汽油）零售价的比例高达五分之四，因此即使原油价格发生很大的变化，对零售价（出泵价格）的影响也比过去更小。 根据上面的内容可知，在零售价格中，原油成本所占份额少，而税收比例高达五分之四，因此很容易推断出结论“税最影响汽油零售价格”，即“如果税上涨，汽油零售价格会大幅上涨”。因此D选项正确，A选项错误。</td></tr><tr><td style='text-align: center; word-wrap: break-word;'>[B]</td><td style='text-align: center; word-wrap: break-word;'>commodity prices rise. 商品价格上涨。</td><td style='text-align: center; word-wrap: break-word;'>【段5】①One more reason not to lose sleep over the rise in oil prices is that, unlike the rises in the 1970s, it has not occurred against the background of general commodity-price inflation and global excess demand. ④In 1973 commodity prices jumped by 70%, and in 1979 by almost 30%. B选项中的commodity prices（商品价格）在段5句①和句④中有提及，但并没有提到商品价格和汽油零售价的关系，无中生有，因此B选项错误。</td></tr><tr><td style='text-align: center; word-wrap: break-word;'>[C]</td><td style='text-align: center; word-wrap: break-word;'>consumption rises. 消耗量增加。</td><td style='text-align: center; word-wrap: break-word;'>【段4】②Energy conservation, a shift to other fuels and a decline in the importance of heavy, energy-intensive industries has reduced oil consumption. 通过C选项中的关键词consumption可以定位到段4句②，原文说的是“能源节约、向其他燃料的转变，以及能源密集型工业重性的下降都减少了石油消耗”。而C选项和题干说的是“如果消耗量增加，汽油零售价格会大幅上涨”。也就是说，原文只提及“……减少了石油消耗”，但“消耗量和汽油零售价格”两者之间的逻辑关系在原文中并没有提及，只是利用常识来干扰，属于无中生有+常识干扰，因此C选项错误。</td></tr><tr><td style='text-align: center; word-wrap: break-word;'>[D]</td><td style='text-align: center; word-wrap: break-word;'>oil taxes rise. 石油税上涨。</td><td style='text-align: center; word-wrap: break-word;'>解析见A选项。</td></tr></table>

①At the end of the day, there's probably little reason to pay attention to our dreams at all unless they keep us from sleeping or "we wake up in a panic,"  $ \underline{\text{Cartwright}} $ says. ②Terrorism, economic uncertainties and general feelings of insecurity have increased people's anxiety. ③ $ \underline{\text{Those suffering from persistent nightmares}} $ should seek help from a therapist. ④ $ \underline{\text{For the rest of us}} $, the brain has its ways of working through bad feelings. ⑤Sleep—or rather dream—on it and you'll feel better in the morning.

①卡特赖特说，说到底，可能根本没什么理由去在意我们的梦，除非它们（梦）使我们无法安睡或“我们从惊恐中醒来”。②恐怖主义、经济不稳定和普遍的不安全感都增加了人们的焦虑。③那些长期受噩梦困扰的人应该寻求治疗专家的帮助。④（而）对其他人来说，大脑有自己处理不良情绪的方法。⑤带着它（不良情绪）睡一觉——或者做个梦——早上（醒来时）你会感觉好多了。

### 35 What advice might  $ \underline{\text{Cartwright}} $ give to  $ \underline{\text{those who sometimes have bad dreams}} $? 卡特赖特可能会给偶尔做噩梦的那些人提什么建议？



<table border=1 style='margin: auto; word-wrap: break-word;'><tr><td colspan="3">题干定位 根据题干中的 Cartwright 可以定位到段4和段5；再根据题干中的 those who sometimes have bad dreams（有时做噩梦的那些人）去原文中找对应，虽然找不到一模一样的内容，但是可以在段5找到它的同义改写 Those suffering from persistent nightmares... For the rest of us... [那些长期受噩梦困扰的人……（而）对其他人来说……]，因为这里的“其他人”就是指“不是长期做噩梦的人，即偶尔做噩梦的人”，因此缩小范围，定位到段5。</td></tr><tr><td style='text-align: center; word-wrap: break-word;'>[A]</td><td style='text-align: center; word-wrap: break-word;'>Lead your life as usual. 像平常一样生活。</td><td style='text-align: center; word-wrap: break-word;'>【段5】③Those suffering from persistent nightmares should seek help from a therapist. ④For the rest of us, the brain has its ways of working through bad feelings. ⑤Sleep—or rather dream—on it and you'll feel better in the morning. 根据上面的题干定位可知，题干中提问的“偶尔做噩梦的那些人”就是段5句④中的“其他人”，那么这之后的自然是正确答案。句④和句⑤说“（而）对其他人来说，大脑有自己处理不良情绪的方法。带着它（不良情绪）睡一觉——或者做个梦——早上（醒来时）你会感觉好多了”。换言之，Cartwright 就是建议这类人“像平常一样生活”，这属于高度概括，因此A选项正确。</td></tr><tr><td style='text-align: center; word-wrap: break-word;'>[B]</td><td style='text-align: center; word-wrap: break-word;'>Seek professional help. 寻求专业人士的帮助。</td><td style='text-align: center; word-wrap: break-word;'>【段5】③Those suffering from persistent nightmares should seek help from a therapist. 根据静姐的“灵魂三问”比对选项和原文. 1 有否？2 否？有！全！选项Seek professional help（寻求专业人士的帮助）与原文段5句③中的seek help from a therapist（寻求治疗专家的帮助）是同义改写。</td></tr><tr><td style='text-align: center; word-wrap: break-word;'></td><td style='text-align: center; word-wrap: break-word;'></td><td style='text-align: center; word-wrap: break-word;'>3 匹配否？不匹配！题干提问的是“those who sometimes have bad dreams (偶尔做噩梦的那些人)”，而原文此处说的是“Those suffering from persistent nightmares (那些长期受噩梦困扰的人)”，B 选项的回答所针对的人群并不是题干中所问的，属于答非所问，所以 B 选项错误。</td></tr><tr><td style='text-align: center; word-wrap: break-word;'>[C]</td><td style='text-align: center; word-wrap: break-word;'>$ \underline{\text{Exercise conscious control}} $.练习有意识的控制。</td><td style='text-align: center; word-wrap: break-word;'>【段4】②Cartwright believes one can  $ \underline{\text{exercise conscious control}} $ over recurring bad dreams.根据静姐的“灵魂三问”比对选项和原文：1 有否？2 全否？有！全！选项 Exercise conscious control（练习有意识的控制）在原文中可以找到。3 匹配否？不匹配！题干提问的是“those who sometimes have bad dreams (偶尔做噩梦的那些人)”，而原文此处说的是针对recurring bad dreams（重复出现的噩梦），C 选项的回答所针对的人群并不是题干中所问的，属于答非所问，所以 C 选项错误。</td></tr><tr><td style='text-align: center; word-wrap: break-word;'>[D]</td><td style='text-align: center; word-wrap: break-word;'>Avoid  $ \underline{\text{anxiety}} $ in the daytime.避免在白天（产生）焦虑。</td><td style='text-align: center; word-wrap: break-word;'>【段5】②Terrorism, economic uncertainties and general feelings of insecurity have increased people's  $ \underline{\text{anxiety}} $.根据静姐的“灵魂三问”比对选项和原文：1 有否？有！选项中的anxiety（焦虑）在原文中可以找到。2 全否？不全！原文表达的是，有几个原因会增加人们的焦虑，但原文中并没有体现“针对偶尔做噩梦的人，要避免在白天（产生）焦虑”，这属于借用原文中的一个词捏造信息，因此 D 选项错误。</td></tr><tr><td colspan="3">如上题，题干中提问的those who sometimes have bad dreams（偶尔做噩梦的那些人）在原文中不能直接找到；但是原文中有说到Those suffering from persistent nightmares（长期受噩梦困扰的那些人），紧接着又说For the rest of us（对其他人来说），即“除了长期受噩梦困扰的人之外的其余的人”，也就是“偶尔做噩梦的人”。这样就找到了题干在原文中的对应。</td></tr></table>





##### 例17：英语二2015年Text1

段1 ①A new study suggests that contrary to  $ \underline{\text{most surveys}} $, people are actually more stressed at  $ \underline{\text{home}} $ than at work. ②Researchers measured people's cortisol, which is a stress marker, while they were at work and while they were at  $ \underline{\text{home}} $ and found it higher at what is supposed to be a place of refuge.

①一项新的研究表明，与大多数调查相反，人们在家时的压力实际上比上班时更大。②研究人员测量了人们在上班时和在家时的皮质醇（一种压力标志）水平，发现在本该是避风港的地方（家里）时人们的皮质醇水平更高。

21 According to  $ \underline{\text{Paragraph 1, most previous surveys}} $ found that  $ \underline{\text{home}} $ _____.根据第一段，大多数之前的调查发现，家_____。

题干中包含明确的段落信息（Paragraph 1）；题干中的 home 在原文中可以找到；题干中的 most previous surveys 对应原文中的 most surveys，属于同义改写。根据这些信息可以定位到段 1。



<table border=1 style='margin: auto; word-wrap: break-word;'><tr><td style='text-align: center; word-wrap: break-word;'>[A]</td><td style='text-align: center; word-wrap: break-word;'>offered greater relaxation than the workplace比工作场所更让人放松</td><td style='text-align: center; word-wrap: break-word;'>【段1】①A new study suggests that contrary to most surveys, people are actually more stressed at home than at work.根据静姐的“灵魂三问”比对选项和原文：1 有否？有！选项中的 than the workplace 是对原文中 than at work 的同义改写，都表示“比工作场所；比工作时”。2 全否？3 匹配？全！匹配！乍一看选项中的 greater relaxation 与段1句①中的 more stressed 相悖，但要注意原文中的 contrary to. 该句中的 A new study... contrary to most surveys 表明“新研究与（之前）大多数调查的结果相反”，新的研究结果是 people are actually more stressed at home than at work（人们在家时的压力实际上比上班时更大），因此可推断出之前大多数调查的结果是“人们在家时的压力比上班时更小”。题干+A选项 home offered greater relaxation than the workplace 是对该推断的同义改写，因此 A 选项正确。</td></tr><tr><td style='text-align: center; word-wrap: break-word;'>[B]</td><td style='text-align: center; word-wrap: break-word;'>was an ideal place for stress measurement是测量压力的理想场所</td><td style='text-align: center; word-wrap: break-word;'>【段1】②Researchers measured people's cortisol, which is a stress marker, while they were at work and while they were at home...根据静姐的“灵魂三问”比对选项和原文：1 有否？有！选项中的 stress 可以在原文中找到，选项中的 measurement 是对原文中 measured 的同义改写，都表示“测量”。2 全否？3 匹配？不全！不匹配！原文只提到了研究者分别在工作场所和家里测量了人们的压力水平，并没有说家是测量压力的理想场所，选项中的 ideal place（理想场所）属于利用原文中出现过的单词来塑造信息；另外，题干问的是“之前的调查（previous surveys）”，选项对应的段1句②描述的是“新研究”的过程与发现，属于答非所问，因此 B 选项错误。</td></tr><tr><td style='text-align: center; word-wrap: break-word;'>[C]</td><td style='text-align: center; word-wrap: break-word;'>generated more stress than the workplace比工作场所产生更多的压力</td><td style='text-align: center; word-wrap: break-word;'>【段1】①A new study suggests that contrary to most surveys, people are actually more stressed at home than at work.根据静姐的“灵魂三问”比对选项和原文：1 有否？有！选项中的 more stress than the workplace 是对原文中的 more stressed... than at work，属于同义改写。</td></tr><tr><td style='text-align: center; word-wrap: break-word;'></td><td style='text-align: center; word-wrap: break-word;'></td><td style='text-align: center; word-wrap: break-word;'>3 匹配否？不匹配！题干问的是 most previous surveys（大多数之前的调查），而选项对应的是 A new study suggests that contrary to most surveys（一项新的研究表明，与大多数调查相反），属于答非所问，因此 C 选项错误。</td></tr><tr><td style='text-align: center; word-wrap: break-word;'>[D]</td><td style='text-align: center; word-wrap: break-word;'>was an unrealistic place for relaxation是一个不切实际的放松场所</td><td style='text-align: center; word-wrap: break-word;'>【段1】①A new study suggests that contrary to most surveys, people are actually more stressed at home than at work. ②Researchers measured people's cortisol, which is stress marker, while they were at work and while they were at home and found it higher at what is supposed to be a place of refuge. 根据静姐的“灵魂三问”比对选项和原文：1 有否？有！选项中的 place for relaxation（放松场所）对应原文中的 place of refuge（避风港），属于同义改写。2 全否？全！原文说的是“研究人员测量了人们的皮质醇水平（一种压力标志），发现在本该是避风港的地方（家里）时人们的皮质醇水平更高”，也就是说，在家时人的压力更大；选项说的是 unrealistic place for relaxation（不切实际的放松场所），与原文意思相近，属于同义改写。3 匹配否？不匹配！题干问的是 most previous surveys（大多数之前的调查），而选项对应的是 A new study suggests that contrary to most surveys（一项新的研究表明，与大多数调查相反），属于答非所问，因此 D 选项错误。</td></tr><tr><td colspan="3">这道题很难，很多同学在题干定位的时候就被卡住了。题干提问的是 most previous surveys（大多数之前的调查），在原文中不能直接找到；但是原文中有说到 A new study（新的研究）与 most surveys（大多数调查）相反，那么这里的 most surveys（大多数调查）既然不是新的研究，那说明它是旧的、之前的，其实就是 most previous surveys（大多数之前的调查），这就找到了题干对应的原文。然后根据“新的研究”与“之前的调查”的相反关系，可以把新研究的内容反过来，就可以知道之前调查的内容了，这就是深度的细节信息的整合，也是解决推断题的关键所在。</td></tr></table>





##### 例18：英语二2014年Text2

段5 ①Knowing the results of Epley's study, it makes sense that many people hate photographs of themselves viscerally—on one level, they don't even recognise the person in the picture as themselves. ② $ \underline{\text{Facebook}} $, therefore,  $ \underline{\text{is a self-enhancer's paradise}} $, where  $ \underline{\text{people}} $ ①了解埃普利的研究结果后，就能理解（为什么）很多人本能地讨厌自己的照片了——在某种程度上，他们甚至没有认出照片里的人是自己。②脸书因此成了一个自我拔高者的天堂，在那里，人们可以只分享（他们）最漂亮的照片，他们才

can share only the most flattering photos, the cream of their wit, style, beauty, intellect and lifestyles. ③It's not that people's profiles are dishonest, says Catalina Toma of Wisconsin-Madison University, "but they portray an idealised version of themselves."

智、风格、美丽、智力和生活方式的精华。③这并不是说人们在个人形象上不诚实，威斯康星大学麦迪逊分校的卡特琳娜·托马说，“而是他们描绘了一个理想版本的自己”。

30 It can be inferred that  $ \underline{\text{Facebook}} $  $ \underline{\text{is a self-enhancer's paradise}} $ because  $ \underline{\text{people can}} $ ____ .可以推断出，脸书是自我拔高者的天堂，因为人们可以。

题干定位 根据题干中的 Facebook/is a self-enhancer's paradise/people can 这些关键信息可以定位到段 5 句②。



<table border=1 style='margin: auto; word-wrap: break-word;'><tr><td style='text-align: center; word-wrap: break-word;'>[A]</td><td style='text-align: center; word-wrap: break-word;'>present their  $ \underline{\text{dishonest profiles}} $ 呈现他们虚假的个人形象</td><td style='text-align: center; word-wrap: break-word;'>【段5】③It's not that people's  $ \underline{\text{profiles}} $ are  $ \underline{\text{dishonest}} $, says Catalina Toma of Wisconsin-Madison University, "but they portray an idealised version of themselves." 根据静姐的“灵魂三问”比对选项和原文：1 有否？有！选项中的 dishonest 和 profiles 在原文中可以找到。2 全否？不全！原文说的是“这并不是说人们在个人形象上不诚实”，而选项说的是“呈现他们虚假的个人形象”，与原文语义相反，反向干扰，因此 A 选项错误。</td></tr><tr><td style='text-align: center; word-wrap: break-word;'>[B]</td><td style='text-align: center; word-wrap: break-word;'>define their traditional  $ \underline{\text{lifestyles}} $ 定义他们传统的生活方式</td><td style='text-align: center; word-wrap: break-word;'>【段5】②Facebook, therefore, is a self-enhancer's paradise, where people can share only the most flattering photos, the cream of their wit, style, beauty, intellect and  $ \underline{\text{lifestyles}} $. 根据静姐的“灵魂三问”比对选项和原文：1 有否？有！选项中的 lifestyles （生活方式）在原文中可以找到。2 全否？不全！句②提到“人们可以只分享（他们）……生活方式的精华”，并未谈到定义他们传统的生活方式，选项利用原文中出现过的词汇捏造信息，因此 B 选项错误。</td></tr><tr><td style='text-align: center; word-wrap: break-word;'>[C]</td><td style='text-align: center; word-wrap: break-word;'>$ \underline{\text{share their intellectual}} $ pursuits 分享他们的智力追求</td><td style='text-align: center; word-wrap: break-word;'>【段5】②Facebook, therefore, is a self-enhancer's paradise, where people can  $ \underline{\text{share}} $ only the most flattering photos, the cream of  $ \underline{\text{their}} $ wit, style, beauty,  $ \underline{\text{intellect}} $ and lifestyles. 根据静姐的“灵魂三问”比对选项和原文：1 有否？有！选项中的 share 在原文中可以找到；选项中的 intellectual （智力的）对应原文中的 intellect （智力），属于同义改写。2 全否？不全！句②提到“人们可以只分享……他们才智……的精华”，即人们分享的都是自己才智方面最优秀的表现，pursuits （追求） ≠ cream （精华），属于偷换概念，因此 C 选项错误。</td></tr><tr><td style='text-align: center; word-wrap: break-word;'>[D]</td><td style='text-align: center; word-wrap: break-word;'>withhold their unflattering sides\n隐瞒他们不讨喜的方面</td><td style='text-align: center; word-wrap: break-word;'>【段5】②Facebook, therefore, is a self-enhancer's paradise, where people can  $ \underline{\text{share only the most flattering}} $ photos, the cream of their wit, style, beauty, intellect and lifestyles.根据静姐的“灵魂三问”比对选项和原文：1 有否？有！选项中的 unflattering 对应原文中的 flattering，二者是同根反义词。2 全否？全！选项中的 withhold their unflattering（隐瞒他们不讨喜的）对应原文中的 share only the most flattering（只分享最好的），属于正话反说的同义改写。3 匹配否？匹配！由句②可知，脸书之所以成了一个自我拔高者的天堂，是因为在脸书人们可以只分享自己最好的一面，能满足自我拔高者的心理；题干+选项是对这个结论的同义改写，因此 D 选项正确。</td></tr></table>





原文中说的是 share only the most flattering photos（只分享最漂亮的照片），正话反说一下，这句话就可以理解为 withhold their unflattering sides（隐瞒他们不讨喜的方面），因此 D 选项正确。其余的错误选项可以通过静姐的“灵魂三问”法来排除。

①President Trump has underlined fossil fuels—especially coal—as the path to economic growth. ②In a recent speech in Iowa, he dismissed wind power as an unreliable energy source. ③But that message did not play well with many  $ \underline{\text{in Iowa}} $, where wind turbines dot the fields and provide 36 percent of the state's electricity generation—and where tech giants like Microsoft are being attracted by the availability of clean energy to power their data centers.

①特朗普总统强调（将）化石燃料——特别是煤炭——作为经济增长的途径。②最近在艾奥瓦州的一次演讲中，他认为风能是一种不可靠的能源，因而不予考虑。③但这一观点并没有得到艾奥瓦州许多民众的认可，那里的风力涡轮机遍布田野，提供了该州36%的发电量——在那里，微软等科技巨头也被可以为其数据中心供电的清洁能源的易获得性所吸引。

28 It can be learned that  $ \underline{\text{in lowa}} $，____，可以了解到，在艾奥瓦州，____。

题干定位 根据题干中的关键词 in lowa（在艾奥瓦州）可以定位到段 4。

word-wrap: break-word;'>[C]</td><td style='text-align: center; word-wrap: break-word;'>tech giants are investing in clean energy科技巨头正在投资清洁能源</td><td style='text-align: center; word-wrap: break-word;'>【段4】③But that message did not play well with many in lowa, where wind turbines dot the fields and provide 36 percent of the state's electricity generation—and where tech giants like Microsoft are being attracted by the availability of clean energy to power their data centers.根据静姐的“灵魂三问”比对选项和原文：1 有否？有！选项中的 tech giants（科技巨头）/clean energy（清洁能源）在原文中可以找到。2 全否？不全！选项 tech giants are investing in clean energy（科技巨头正在投资清洁能源）与原文 tech giants like Microsoft are being attracted by the availability of clean energy（微软等科技巨头被清洁能源的易获得性所吸引）不符，“被清洁能源的易获得性吸引”≠“投资清洁能源”，属于推断过度，因此C选项错误。</td></tr><tr><td style='text-align: center; ##### 例20：2006年Text2

①The tourist streams are not entirely separate.

②The sightseers who come by bus—and often take in Warwick Castle and Blenheim Palace on the side—don't usually see the plays, and some of them are even surprised to find a theatre in Stratford. ③However, the playgoers do manage a little sight-seeing along with their playgoing. ④It is the playgoers, the RSC contends, who bring in much of the town's revenue because they spend the night (some of them four or five nights) pouring cash into the hotels and restaurants. ⑤The sightseers can take in everything and get out of town by nightfall.

①游客并没有完全分流。②乘大巴过来的观光客，经常顺道去参观华威城堡和布伦海姆宫，但通常不会去看戏，他们中的一些人甚至会惊讶地发现斯特拉特福德镇居然还有一家剧院。③然而，来看戏剧的人的确会在看戏之余设法抽出时间看看景点。④皇家莎士比亚剧团声称，正是来看戏的游客带来了小镇的大部分收入，因为他们（通常在此）过夜（他们中一些人会待四到五个晚上），将大把的钱花在旅馆和餐馆里。⑤观光客会在夜幕降临前游览完所有景点并离开小镇。

### It can be inferred from  $ \underline{\text{Paragraph 3}} $ that 从第三段可以推断

题干定位 根据题干中明确的段落信息定位到段3。



<table border="1" style="margin: auto; word-wrap: break-word;"><tr><td style="text-align: center; word-wrap: break-word;">[A]</td><td style="text-align: center; word-wrap: break-word;">the sightseers cannot visit the Castle and the Palace separately. 观光客不可以分别参观城堡和宫殿。</td><td style="text-align: center; word-wrap: break-word;">【段3】①The tourist streams are not entirely separate. ②The sightseers who come by bus—and often take in Warwick Castle and Blenheim Palace on the side—don't usually see the plays, and some of them are even surprised to find a theatre in Stratford. 根据静姐的“灵魂三问”比对选项和原文：1 有否？有！选项中的 sightseers/Castle/Palace 在原文中都可以找到，并且选项中的 separately 对应原文中的 separate，属于同根词的同义改写。2 全否？不全！原文表达的是“游客并没有完全分流。乘大巴过来的观光客经常顺道去参观城堡和宫殿”；选项表达的是“观光客不可以分别参观城堡和宫殿”，A选项杂糅了句①和句②的内容，与原文内容不符，属于曲解原文，因此A选项错误。</td></tr><tr><td style="text-align: center; word-wrap: break-word;">[B]</td><td style="text-align: center; word-wrap: break-word;">the playgoers spend more money than the sightseers. 看戏的游客比观光客花的钱更多。</td><td style="text-align: center; word-wrap: break-word;">【段3】②The sightseers who come by bus—and often take in Warwick Castle and Blenheim Palace on the side—don't usually see the plays, and some of them are even surprised to find a theatre in Stratford. ③However, the playgoers do manage a little sight-seeing along with their playgoing. ④It is the playgoers, the RSC contends, who bring in much of the town's revenue because they spend the night (some of them four or five nights) pouring cash into the hotels and restaurants. ⑤The sightseers can take in everything and get out of town by nightfall.句②和句⑤表明观光客不看戏，停留时间短，花费少；句③和句④则表明看戏的游客既看戏也观光，停留时间长，花费多。所以看戏的游客比观光客花的钱多，因此B选项正确，这是对原文的高度概括。</td></tr><tr><td style="text-align: center; word-wrap: break-word;">[C]</td><td style="text-align: center; word-wrap: break-word;">the sightseers do more shopping than the playgoers. 观光客比看戏的游客购物更多。</td><td style="text-align: center; word-wrap: break-word;">【段3】②The sightseers who come by bus—and often take in Warwick Castle and Blenheim Palace on the side—don't usually see the plays... ④It is the playgoers, the RSC contends, who bring in much of the town's revenue because they spend the night (some of them four or five nights) pouring cash into the hotels and restaurants. 根据静姐的“灵魂三问”比对选项和原文：1 有否？有！选项中的 the sightseers 和 the playgoers 在原文中可以找到。2 全否？不全！原文只是说“观光客通常不会去看戏，而那些看戏的游客带</td></tr><tr><td style="text-align: center; word-wrap: break-word;"></td><td style="text-align: center; word-wrap: break-word;"></td><td style="text-align: center; word-wrap: break-word;">来了小镇的大部分收入，因为他们通常在小镇过夜，将大把的钱花在旅馆和餐馆里”，并没有提及与shopping相关的内容，更没有将观光客和看戏的游客的购物作对比。选项利用原文中出现的个别单词捏造出原文没有提及的内容，属于捏造信息，因此C选项错误。</td></tr><tr><td style="text-align: center; word-wrap: break-word;">[D]</td><td style="text-align: center; word-wrap: break-word;">$ \underline{\text{the playgoers}} $ go to no other places in town than the theater.看戏的游客除了去剧院，不去镇上其他地方。</td><td style="text-align: center; word-wrap: break-word;">【段3】③However， $ \underline{\text{the playgoers}} $ do manage a little sight-seeing along with their playgoing.根据静姐的“灵魂三问”比对选项和原文：1 有否？有！选项中的the playgoers在原文中可以找到。2 全否？不全！原文说的是“来看戏剧的人的确会在看戏之余设法抽出时间看看景点”；选项说的是“看戏的游客除了去剧院，不去镇上其他地方”，属于反向干扰，因此D选项错误。</td></tr><tr><td colspan="3">注意A和C选项都是利用原文中出现过的信息，再加上捏造的错误内容创造的干扰项；D选项是对原文的反向干扰，把原文内容说反了，B选项正确，是对于原文的高度概括。</td></tr></table>




##### 例21：英语二2011年Text 3

①Economic condition was only a stimulus for the trend toward efficient living. ②The phrase "less is more" was actually first popularized by a German, the architect Ludwig Mies van der Rohe, who like other people associated with  $ \underline{\text{the Bauhaus}} $, a school of design, emigrated to the United States before World War II and took up posts at American architecture schools. ③These designers came to exert enormous influence on the course of American architecture, but none more so than Mies.

①经济状况只是这种高效生活趋势（形成）的一个刺激因素。②实际上，“少即是多”这句话首先是由一位名叫路德维希·密斯 凡德罗的德国建筑师推广而来的，像其他与包豪斯建筑学院相关的设计师一样，他在“二战”之前移居到美国，并在美国多个建筑学院任职。③这些设计师们对美国建筑的发展产生了巨大的影响，但其中影响最大的是密斯。

### 32 Which of the following can be inferred from  $ \underline{\text{Paragraph 3}} $ about  $ \underline{\text{the Bauhaus}} $? 根据第三段，可以推断出下列哪个关于包豪斯的选项是正确的？

##### 题干定位 根据题干中明确的段落信息和关键词 the Bauhaus（包豪斯）定位到段3。



<table border=1 style='margin: auto; word-wrap: break-word;'><tr><td style='text-align: center; word-wrap: break-word;'>[A]</td><td style='text-align: center; word-wrap: break-word;'>It was founded by  $ \underline{\text{Ludwig Mies van der Rohe}} $.它由路德维希·密斯 凡德罗创建。</td><td style='text-align: center; word-wrap: break-word;'>【段3】②The phrase “less is more” was actually first popularized by a German, the architect  $ \underline{\text{Ludwig Mies van der Rohe}} $, who like other people associated with the Bauhaus, a school of design, emigrated to the United States before World War II and took up posts at American architecture schools.根据静姐的“灵魂三问”比对选项和原文：</td></tr><tr><td rowspan="2">[B]</td><td rowspan="2">Its designing concept was affected by World War II.它的设计理念受二战影响。</td><td style='text-align: center; word-wrap: break-word;'>1 有否？有！选项中的 Ludwig Mies van der Rohe 在原文中可以找到。2 全否？不全！选项 It was founded by Ludwig Mies van der Rohe（它由路德维希·密斯·凡德罗创建）与原文 Ludwig Mies van der Rohe, who like other people associated with the Bauhaus（路德维希·密斯·凡德罗，像其他与包豪斯建筑学院相关的设计师一样）内容不符，相关≠创建，属于偷换概念，因此 A 选项错误。</td></tr><tr><td style='text-align: center; word-wrap: break-word;'>【段3】②...a school of design, emigrated to the United States before World War II and took up posts at American architecture schools.根据静姐的“灵魂三问”比对选项和原文：1 有否？有！选项中的 World War II 在原文中可以找到；选项中的 designing 对应原文中的 design，都表示“设计”，属于同义改写。2 全否？不全！原文说的是，路德维希·密斯·凡德罗像其他与包豪斯建筑学院相关的设计师一样，在“二战”之前移居到美国，并未提及包豪斯的设计理念受到“二战”的影响，选项属于捏造信息，因此 B 选项错误。</td></tr><tr><td style='text-align: center; word-wrap: break-word;'>[C]</td><td style='text-align: center; word-wrap: break-word;'>Most American architects used to be associated with it.大部分美国建筑师都曾与它有关联。</td><td style='text-align: center; word-wrap: break-word;'>【段3】②...who like other people associated with the Bauhaus, a school of design, emigrated to the United States before World War II and took up posts at American architecture schools.根据静姐的“灵魂三问”比对选项和原文：1 有否？有！选项中的 associated with（与……有关联）在原文中可以找到，选项中的 it 指代的就是题干中的 the Bauhaus（包豪斯）。在原文中可以找到。2 全否？不全！原文 other people associated with the Bauhaus（其他与包豪斯建筑学院相关的设计师）与选项 Most American architects used to be associated with it（大部分美国建筑师都曾与它有关联）不符，其他设计师≠大部分美国建筑师，属于偷换概念，因此 C 选项错误。</td></tr><tr><td style='text-align: center; word-wrap: break-word;'>[D]</td><td style='text-align: center; word-wrap: break-word;'>It had a great influence upon American architecture.它对美国的建筑有巨大的影响。</td><td style='text-align: center; word-wrap: break-word;'>【段3】②The phrase “less is more” was actually first popularized by a German, the architect Ludwig Mies van der Rohe, who like other people associated with the Bauhaus, a school of design, emigrated to the United States before World War II and took up posts at American architecture schools.③These designers came to exert enormous influence on the</td></tr><tr><td style='text-align: center; word-wrap: break-word;'></td><td style='text-align: center; word-wrap: break-word;'></td><td style='text-align: center; word-wrap: break-word;'>course of  $ \underline{\text{American architecture}} $, but none more so than Mies. 根据静姐的“灵魂三问”比对选项和原文：1 有否？有！选项中的 American architecture（美国的建筑）在原文中可以直接找到。2 全否？全！选项中的 had a great influence upon（对……有巨大的影响）是对原文 exert enormous influence on（对……施加了巨大的影响）的同义改写；选项中的 American architecture（美国的建筑）与原文中的 the course of American architecture（美国建筑的发展）虽然在表述上略有不同，但“对美国建筑发展的影响”也就是“对美国建筑的影响”，意思相同。3 匹配否？匹配！题干问的是有关 Bauhaus（包豪斯）的情况，选项中的 It 指的就是题干中的包豪斯，即选项的意思是“包豪斯对美国的建筑有巨大的影响”。原文中句③说的是“These designers（这些设计师）对美国建筑产生了巨大的影响”，并且在上文的句②中还说明“这些设计师都是与包豪斯这个设计学校有关的”，把这两句话合并在一起理解，即“包豪斯间接对美国的建筑有巨大的影响”。虽然选项内容不能与原文完全对应，但表述的大致方向基本一致，符合题干所问，因此 D 选项正确。注意：D 选项虽然不是“完美的”选项，但是所有选项中 D 选项的错误最轻，本着“择优录取”的原则，所以 D 选项是正确选项。</td></tr><tr><td colspan="3">这道题非常易错，因为得正确理解了句②长难句之后，才能解决选项 A、B、C。注意 D 选项，虽然它是正确答案，但它并不是一个完美的选项，详见讲解。</td></tr></table>








##### 例22: 2006年 Text 3

段①When  $ \underline{\text{prehistoric}} $ man arrived in new parts of the world, something strange happened to the  $ \underline{\text{large animals}} $: they suddenly became  $ \underline{\text{extinct}} $. ②Smaller species survived. ③The large, slow-growing animals were easy game, and were quickly hunted to  $ \underline{\text{extinction}} $. ④Now something similar could be happening in the oceans.

①当史前人类到达世界的新区域时，奇怪的事情发生了大型动物身上：它们突然灭绝了。②较小的物种幸存下来了。③大型的生长缓慢的动物是容易被捕获的猎物，很快被猎杀到灭绝。④现在，类似的事情可能正发生在海洋中。

### 31 The  $ \underline{extinction} $ of  $ \underline{large} $  $ \underline{prehistoric} $  $ \underline{animals} $ is noted to suggest that 提到史前大型动物的灭绝是为了表明

题干定位 题干中的 extinction/large/prehistoric/animals 可以在原文中直接找到；题干中的名词 extinction 还对应原文中的形容词 extinct，都表示“灭绝”。根据这些关键词，可以定位到段 1。



<table border=1 style='margin: auto; word-wrap: break-word;'><tr><td rowspan="2">[A]</td><td style='text-align: center; word-wrap: break-word;'>changing environment.</td><td style='text-align: center; word-wrap: break-word;'>A 选项中的 changing environment（变化的环境）对应原文中的</td></tr><tr><td style='text-align: center; word-wrap: break-word;'>大型动物容易受到环境变化的影响。</td><td style='text-align: center; word-wrap: break-word;'>new parts of the world（世界的新区域），算同义改写。但是 were vulnerable to（容易受到……的影响）在文中没有提及，属于捏造信息，因此 A 选项错误。</td></tr><tr><td rowspan="2">[B]</td><td style='text-align: center; word-wrap: break-word;'>small species survived as large animals disappeared.</td><td style='text-align: center; word-wrap: break-word;'>【段1】①When prehistoric man arrived in new parts of the world, something strange happened to the large animals: they suddenly became extinct. ②Smaller species survived. ③The large, slow-growing animals were easy game, and were quickly hunted to extinction. B 选项是最易错选的。选项中是 small species（小型物种），原文中是 Smaller species（较小、更小的物种），细节不一致，属于曲解原文，这是错误一。</td></tr><tr><td style='text-align: center; word-wrap: break-word;'>小型物种幸存了下来，因为大型动物消失了。</td><td style='text-align: center; word-wrap: break-word;'>连词 as 有多种含义，可以表示原因“因为”，也可以表示时间“当……时候”或表示方式“按照……方式”等，但是无论选项中的 as 表示什么含义都不对，因为选项中的前后两件事（小型物种幸存/大型动物消失）在原文中并没有提及有因果关系或任何其他逻辑关系，属于强加关联，这是错误二。因此 B 选项错误。</td></tr><tr><td rowspan="3">[C]</td><td style='text-align: center; word-wrap: break-word;'>其他含义，见右侧详解）</td><td style='text-align: center; word-wrap: break-word;'>【段1】①When prehistoric man arrived in new parts of the world, something strange happened to the large animals: they suddenly became extinct. ②Smaller species survived. ③The large, slow-growing animals were easy game, and were quickly hunted to extinction. ④Now something similar could be happening in the oceans.</td></tr><tr><td style='text-align: center; word-wrap: break-word;'>large sea animals may face the same threat today.</td><td style='text-align: center; word-wrap: break-word;'>根据题干定位到段1句①～③，原文讲的是“史前人类到达的地方，大型动物灭绝，较小的物种幸存下来”。之后句④指出“现在，类似的事情可能正发生在海洋中”，下文也都是在讲述海洋生物濒临灭绝，所以提到“史前大型动物的灭绝”就是为了引出文章主题——大型海洋生物可能面临同样的威胁，因此 C 选项正确。</td></tr><tr><td style='text-align: center; word-wrap: break-word;'>如今大型海洋动物可能面临同样的威胁。</td><td style='text-align: center; word-wrap: break-word;'>【段1】③The large, slow-growing animals were easy game, and were quickly hunted to extinction.</td></tr><tr><td rowspan="2">[D]</td><td style='text-align: center; word-wrap: break-word;'>slow-growing fish outlive fast-growing ones.</td><td style='text-align: center; word-wrap: break-word;'>原文说的是“大型的生长缓慢的动物是容易被捕获的猎物，很快被猎杀到灭绝”；而选项与原文相同的就只有一个词 slow-growing，选项中的 outlive 和 fast-growing ones 原文没有提及，属于捏造信息，因此 D 选项错误。</td></tr><tr><td style='text-align: center; word-wrap: break-word;'>生长缓慢的鱼类比生长快速的鱼类活得更长。</td><td style='text-align: center; word-wrap: break-word;'>正确选项 C 的内容在原文中并不能直接找到，但是可以根据原文的句④ Now something similar could be happening in the oceans（现在，类似的事情可能正发生在海洋中），再结合上文说过的内容“大型动物灭绝”，则可以整合出正确答案的内容“大型海洋动物可能面临同样的威胁”。B 选项最易错选，错误在于两点，详见讲解。</td></tr></table>

##### 例23：英语—2012年Text3

<div style="text-align: center;"><img src="https://pplines-online.bj.bcebos.com/deploy/official/paddleocr/pp-ocr-vl-16-online//8eff2f4a-94b3-4234-a7d5-c1a70783d850/markdown_4/imgs/img_in_image_box_154_159_222_185.jpg?authorization=bce-auth-v1%2FALTAKDN8mY5KlNI7zaRpLmOqrw%2F2026-06-22T15%3A15%3A53Z%2F-1%2F%2F89530731c758b81e6cbca8303c6a69ab3fbe9169c7999f1bd452c8e42f8e2eac" alt="Image" width="5%" />

①Consequently, discovery claims should be thought of as protoscience. ②Similar to newly staked mining claims, they are full of potential. ③But it takes collective scrutiny and acceptance to transform a discovery claim into a mature discovery. ④This is the  $ \underline{\text{credibility process}} $, through which the individual researcher's me, here, now becomes the community's anyone, anywhere, anytime. ⑤Objective knowledge is the goal, not the starting point.

①因此，发现声明应该被视作科学雏形。②与新宣布的采矿权声明类似，它们颇具潜力。③但是它（发现声明）需要经过集体审查和认可才能转变为成熟的发现。④这就是取信过程，通过这个过程，单个研究者的“我”“此地”和“此时”转变成科学界的“任何人”“任何地点”和“任何时间”。⑤客观知识是目标，而非起点。

### 32 It can be inferred from  $ \underline{\text{Paragraph 2}} $ that  $ \underline{\text{credibility process}} $ requires 根据第二段可以推知取信过程需要

根据题干中明确的段落信息和关键词 credibility process 定位到段2。



<table border="1" style="margin: auto; word-wrap: break-word;"><tr><td style="text-align: center; word-wrap: break-word;">[A]</td><td style="text-align: center; word-wrap: break-word;">$ \underline{\text{strict inspection}} $.严格的审查。</td><td style="text-align: center; word-wrap: break-word;">【段2】③But it takes collective  $ \underline{\text{scrutiny}} $ and acceptance to transform a discovery claim into a mature discovery.根据静姐的“灵魂三问”比对选项和原文：1 有否？2 全否？有！全！选项 strict inspection（严格的审查）对应原文段2句③中的scrutiny（详细审查），属于同义改写。3 匹配否？不匹配！段2句③提到发现声明需要经过集体审查和认可才能转变为成熟的发现，题干+选项说“取信过程需要严格的审查”，忽略了取信过程还需要得到集体的认可，属于以偏概全，因此A选项错误。</td></tr><tr><td style="text-align: center; word-wrap: break-word;">[B]</td><td style="text-align: center; word-wrap: break-word;">$ \underline{\text{shared efforts}} $.共同的努力。</td><td style="text-align: center; word-wrap: break-word;">【段2】③But it takes  $ \underline{\text{collective scrutiny and acceptance}} $ to transform a discovery claim into a mature discovery.④This is the credibility process, through which the individual researcher's me, here, now becomes the community's anyone, anywhere, anytime.根据静姐的“灵魂三问”比对选项和原文：1 有否？有！选项中的shared（共同的）对应原文中的collective（集体的），属于同义改写。2 全否？全！原文中的collective scrutiny and acceptance（集体审查和认可）对应选项shared efforts（共同的努力），前者属于后者，同义改写。</td></tr><tr><td style="text-align: center; word-wrap: break-word;"></td><td style="text-align: center; word-wrap: break-word;"></td><td style="text-align: center; word-wrap: break-word;">3 匹配否？匹配！原文句④指出“这就是取信过程”，其中 This 指代的就是句③中所说的“经过集体审查和认可”，符合题干所问，因此 B 选项正确。</td></tr><tr><td style="text-align: center; word-wrap: break-word;">[C]</td><td style="text-align: center; word-wrap: break-word;">$ \underline{\text{individual}} $ wisdom.个人的智慧。</td><td style="text-align: center; word-wrap: break-word;">【段2】④This is the credibility process, through which the  $ \underline{\text{individual}} $ researcher's me, here, now becomes the community's anyone, anywhere, anytime.根据静姐的“灵魂三问”比对选项和原文：1 有否？有！选项中的 individual（个人的）在原文中可以找到。2 全否？3 匹配否？不全！不匹配！段2句④提到，在取信过程中，单个研究者的“我”“此地”和“此时”转变成科学界的“任何人”“任何地点”和“任何时间”。由此可知，原文强调取信过程中“集体”的作用。题干+选项说“取信过程需要个人的智慧”，与原文不符，属于曲解原文，因此 C 选项错误。</td></tr><tr><td style="text-align: center; word-wrap: break-word;">[D]</td><td style="text-align: center; word-wrap: break-word;">persistent innovation.不断的创新。</td><td style="text-align: center; word-wrap: break-word;">根据静姐的“灵魂三问”比对选项和原文：1 有否？没有！选项 persistent innovation（不断的创新）在原文中没有提及，属于无中生有+常识干扰，因此 D 选项错误。</td></tr><tr><td colspan="3">B 选项 shared efforts（共同的努力）对应原文的 collective scrutiny and acceptance（集体审查和认可），换种方式表达，就是推断题的解题关键。A 选项最易错选，虽然 A 选项 strict inspection（严格的审查）是对原文 scrutiny（仔细观察，详细审查）的同义改写，但是遗漏了原文中表达的重点信息 collective（集体的，共同的），因此 A 选项错误。</td></tr></table>




##### 例24：英语二2016年Text4

① $ \underline{\text{Young people}} $ who are still getting started in life  $ \underline{\text{were more likely}} $ than older adults  $ \underline{\text{to}} $ prioritize personal fulfillment in their work, to believe they will advance their careers most by regularly changing jobs, to favor communities with more public services and a faster pace of life, to agree that couples should be financially secure before getting married or having children, and to maintain that children are best served by two parents working outside the home, the survey found.

①该调查发现，仍处于人生起步阶段的年轻人相比年龄稍长的成年人更可能优先考虑在工作中的个人成就感，更可能相信通过定期更换工作能在最大程度上推动职业发展，更可能喜欢公共服务更多、生活节奏更快的社区，更可能赞成夫妻在结婚或生子前应该有经济保障，更可能认为孩子最好由在外工作的父母来抚养。

37 It can be learned from  $ \underline{\text{Paragraph 3}} $ that  $ \underline{\text{young people}} $  $ \underline{\text{tend to}} $ ____ .从第三段可知，年轻人往往_____。



<table border=1 style='margin: auto; word-wrap: break-word;'><tr><td style='text-align: center; word-wrap: break-word;'>题干定位</td><td style='text-align: center; word-wrap: break-word;'>题干中包含明确的段落信息（Paragraph 3）；题干中的 young people 在原文中可以找到；题干中的 tend to（往往）对应原文 were more likely... to（更可能），属于同义改写。根据这些信息可以定位到段3。</td></tr><tr><td style='text-align: center; word-wrap: break-word;'>[A]</td><td style='text-align: center; word-wrap: break-word;'>【段3】①Young people... were more likely... to believe they will advance their careers most by regularly changing jobs, to favor communities with more public services and a faster pace of life... 根据静姐的“灵魂三问”比对选项和原文：1 有否？喜欢较慢的生活节奏有！选项中的 favor 在原文中可以找到；选项中的 a... life pace 对应原文 a... pace of life，属于同义改写，均表示“生活节奏”。2 全否？不全！原文说的是 favor communities with... a faster pace of life（喜欢生活节奏更快的社区），选项说的是 favor a slower life pace（喜欢较慢的生活节奏），属于反向干扰，因此 A 选项错误。</td></tr><tr><td style='text-align: center; word-wrap: break-word;'>[B]</td><td style='text-align: center; word-wrap: break-word;'>【段3】①Young people... were more likely... to believe they will advance their careers most by regularly changing jobs... 根据静姐的“灵魂三问”比对选项和原文：1 有否？hold an occupation longer 有！选项中的 occupation 对应原文 jobs，属于同义改写，都表示“工作”。2 全否？不全！原文说的是 regularly changing jobs（定期更换工作），选项说的是 hold an occupation longer（更长久地从事一份工作），属于反向干扰，因此 B 选项错误。</td></tr><tr><td style='text-align: center; word-wrap: break-word;'>[C]</td><td style='text-align: center; word-wrap: break-word;'>【段3】①Young people... were more likely... to agree that couples should be financially secure before getting married or having children... 根据静姐的“灵魂三问”比对选项和原文：1 有否？attach importance to pre-marital finance 有！选项中的 pre-marital 对应原文中的 before getting married, finance 对应原文中的 financially，属于同义改写。2 全否？3 匹配否？全！匹配！原文句①指出 Young people... were more likely... to agree that couples should be financially secure before getting married（年轻人……更可能……赞成夫妻在结婚前应该有经济保障），即 young people tend to attach importance to pre-marital finance（年轻人往往重视婚前财务状况），题干 + 选项是对原文句①的同义改写，因此 C 选项正确。</td></tr></table>



<table border=1 style='margin: auto; word-wrap: break-word;'><tr><td style='text-align: center; word-wrap: break-word;'>[D]</td><td style='text-align: center; word-wrap: break-word;'>give  $ \underline{\text{priority}} $ to childcare  $ \underline{\text{outside the home}} $优先考虑在外面托管孩子</td><td style='text-align: center; word-wrap: break-word;'>【段3】①Young people who are still getting started in life were more likely than older adults to  $ \underline{\text{prioritize}} $ personal fulfillment in their work... and to maintain that children are best served by two parents working  $ \underline{\text{outside the home}} $, the survey found.根据静姐的“灵魂三问”比对选项和原文：1 有否？有！选项中的 outside the home 在原文中可以找到，选项中的 priority（优先级）对应原文中的 prioritize（优先考虑），属于同义改写。2 全否？不全！原文中 prioritize（优先考虑）的对象是“在工作中的个人成就感”，而不是选项中的“在外面托管孩子”；且原文 outside the home 修饰的是“工作的父母”，并没有提到选项中的 childcare（照顾孩子）。选项属于拼凑原文 + 捏造信息，因此 D 选项错误。</td></tr><tr><td colspan="3">推断题和细节题一样，有平行结构（并列结构）的地方易出题。定位句中 be more likely to do sth.（更有可能做某事）这一词组后，平行并列了 5 个 to do 的词组，4 个选项正好对应其中的 4 点进行出题。正确答案 C 虽然不能在原文中直接找到，但是是对原文的同义改写。</td></tr></table>

## 三、观点题

#### 自测

##### 例25：2005年Text3

<div style="text-align: center;"><img src="https://pplines-online.bj.bcebos.com/deploy/official/paddleocr/pp-ocr-vl-16-online//85f68b2f-07d0-4cd2-8292-78786da596dc/markdown_2/imgs/img_in_image_box_102_1034_170_1092.jpg?authorization=bce-auth-v1%2FALTAKDN8mY5KlNI7zaRpLmOqrw%2F2026-06-22T15%3A15%3A32Z%2F-1%2F%2Ff73bcd40026926327788d805ce3fa0a4215d7be4d583423f9330485da0a221b5" alt="Image" width="5%" />

<div style="text-align: center;"><img src="https://pplines-online.bj.bcebos.com/deploy/official/paddleocr/pp-ocr-vl-16-online//85f68b2f-07d0-4cd2-8292-78786da596dc/markdown_2/imgs/img_in_image_box_102_1034_170_1092.jpg?authorization=bce-auth-v1%2FALTAKDN8mY5KlNI7zaRpLmOqrw%2F2026-06-22T15%3A15%3A32Z%2F-1%2F%2Ff73bcd40026926327788d805ce3fa0a4215d7be4d583423f9330485da0a221b5" alt="Image" width="5%" />

段1 $ ^{①} $

</div>


</div>


① Of all the components of a good night's sleep, dreams seem to be least within our control.

② In dreams, a window opens into a world where logic is suspended and dead people speak. ③ A century ago, Freud formulated his revolutionary theory that dreams were the disguised shadows of our unconscious desires and fears; by the late 1970s, neurologists had switched to thinking of them as just "mental noise" —the random byproducts of the neural-repair work that goes on during sleep. ④ Now researchers suspect that dreams are part of the mind's emotional thermostat, regulating moods while the brain is "off-line." ⑤ And one leading authority says that these intensely powerful mental events can be not only harnessed but actually brought under conscious control, to help us sleep and feel better. ⑥ "It's your dream," says Rosalind Cartwright, chair of psychology at Chicago's Medical Center. ⑦ "If you don't like it, change it."

31. Researchers have come to believe that dreams

[A] can be modified in their courses.

[B] are susceptible to emotional changes.

[C] reflect our innermost desires and fears.

[D] are a random outcome of neural repairs.

##### 例26：英语一2011年Text1

① Devoted concertgoers who reply that recordings are no substitute for live performance are missing the point. ② For the time, attention, and money of the art-loving public, classical instrumentalists must compete not only with opera houses, dance troupes, theater companies, and museums, but also with the recorded performances of the great classical musicians of the 20th century. ③ These recordings are cheap, available everywhere, and very often much higher in artistic quality than today's live performances; moreover, they can be "consumed" at a time and place of the listener's choosing. ④ The widespread availability of such recordings has thus brought about a crisis in the institution of the traditional classical concert.

23. The author believes that the devoted concertgoers

[A] ignore the expenses of live performances.

[B] reject most kinds of recorded performances.

[C] exaggerate the variety of live performances.

[D] overestimate the value of live performances.

① And this process need not be left to the unconscious. ② Cartwright believes one can exercise conscious control over recurring bad dreams. ③ As soon as you awaken, identify what is upsetting about the dream. ④ Visualize how you would like it to end instead; the next time it occurs, try to wake up just enough to control its course. ⑤ With much practice people can learn to, literally, do it in their sleep.

[A] waking up in time is essential to the ridding of bad dreams.

[B] visualizing bad dreams helps bring them under control.

[C] dreams should be left to their natural progression.

##### 例30：英语二2011年Text1

<div style="text-align: center;"><img src="https://pplines-online.bj.bcebos.com/deploy/official/paddleocr/pp-ocr-vl-16-online//85f68b2f-07d0-4cd2-8292-78786da596dc/markdown_4/imgs/img_in_image_box_87_1054_159_1111.jpg?authorization=bce-auth-v1%2FALTAKDN8mY5KlNI7zaRpLmOqrw%2F2026-06-22T15%3A15%3A34Z%2F-1%2F%2F3945833294a0cffce6ed22b8b22893bc0c7e3421c008219dbd3374b41a9229b8" alt="Image" width="6%" />

<div style="text-align: center;"><img src="https://pplines-online.bj.bcebos.com/deploy/official/paddleocr/pp-ocr-vl-16-online//85f68b2f-07d0-4cd2-8292-78786da596dc/markdown_4/imgs/img_in_image_box_87_1054_159_1111.jpg?authorization=bce-auth-v1%2FALTAKDN8mY5KlNI7zaRpLmOqrw%2F2026-06-22T15%3A15%3A34Z%2F-1%2F%2F3945833294a0cffce6ed22b8b22893bc0c7e3421c008219dbd3374b41a9229b8" alt="Image" width="6%" />

段3 $ ^{①} $

</div>


</div>


① The researchers from Ohio University used a database that covered more than 10,000 firms and more than 64,000 different directors between 1989 and 2004. ② Then they simply checked which directors stayed from one proxy statement to the next. ③ The most likely reason for departing a board was age, so the researchers concentrated on those "surprise" disappearances by directors under the age of 70. ④ They found that after a surprise departure, the probability that the company will subsequently have to restate earnings increases by nearly 20%. ⑤ The likelihood of being named in a federal class-action lawsuit also increases, and the stock is likely to perform worse. ⑥ The effect tended to be larger for larger firms. ⑦ Although a correlation between them leaving and subsequent bad performance at the firm is suggestive, it does not mean that such directors are always jumping off a sinking ship. ⑧ Often they "trade up," leaving riskier, smaller firms for larger and more stable firms.

23. According to the researchers from Ohio University, after an outside director's surprise departure, the firm is likely to _____

[A] become more stable

[B] report increased earnings

[C] do less well in the stock market

[D] perform worse in lawsuits

##### 例32：英语二2019年Text1

<div style="text-align: center;"><img src="https://pplines-online.bj.bcebos.com/deploy/official/paddleocr/pp-ocr-vl-16-online//54b730ea-3c41-4517-afe5-b2e20d6bd190/markdown_0/imgs/img_in_image_box_168_906_237_924.jpg?authorization=bce-auth-v1%2FALTAKDN8mY5KlNI7zaRpLmOqrw%2F2026-06-22T15%3A15%3A53Z%2F-1%2F%2Fc2c92d92a699d34f0307042b3ce03b6480c10385ca02553d040c4ce0d82ebc9c" alt="Image" width="5%" />

<div style="text-align: center;"><img src="https://pplines-online.bj.bcebos.com/deploy/official/paddleocr/pp-ocr-vl-16-online//54b730ea-3c41-4517-afe5-b2e20d6bd190/markdown_0/imgs/img_in_image_box_168_906_237_924.jpg?authorization=bce-auth-v1%2FALTAKDN8mY5KlNI7zaRpLmOqrw%2F2026-06-22T15%3A15%3A53Z%2F-1%2F%2Fc2c92d92a699d34f0307042b3ce03b6480c10385ca02553d040c4ce0d82ebc9c" alt="Image" width="5%" />

～

</div>


</div>


① Viewed in this light, guilt is an opportunity. ② Work by Tina Malti, a psychology professor at the University of Toronto, suggests that guilt may compensate for an emotional deficiency. ③ In a number of studies, Malti and others have shown that guilt and sympathy may represent different pathways to cooperation and sharing. ④ Some kids who are low in sympathy may make up for that shortfall by experiencing more guilt, which can rein in their nastier impulses. ⑤ And vice versa: High sympathy can substitute for low guilt.

24. Malta and others have shown that cooperation and sharing _____

[A] may be the outcome of impulsive acts

[B] may help correct emotional deficiencies

[D] can result from either sympathy or guilt

##### 例33：2006年Text1

① In spite of "endless talk of difference," American society is an amazing machine for homogenizing people. ② There is "the democratizing uniformity of dress and discourse, and the casualness and absence of deference" characteristic of popular culture. ③ People are absorbed into

“a culture of consumption” launched by the 19th-century department stores that offered “vast arrays of goods in an elegant atmosphere. ④ Instead of intimate shops catering to a knowledgeable elite” these were stores “anyone could enter, regardless of class or background. ⑤ This turned shopping into a public and democratic act.” ⑥ The mass media, advertising and sports are other forces for homogenization.

[A] played a role in the spread of popular culture.

[B] became intimate shops for common consumers.

[C] satisfied the needs of a knowledgeable elite.

[D] owed its emergence to the culture of consumption.

##### 例34：2004年Text4

①"Schools have always been in a society where practical is more important than intellectual," says education writer Diane Ravitch. ②"Schools could be a counterbalance." ③Ravitch's latest book, Left Back: A Century of Failed School Reforms, traces the roots of anti-intellectualism in our schools, concluding they are anything but a counterbalance to the American distaste for intellectual pursuits.

#### 精讲

扫码关注

免费网课+无水印PDF

观点题考查的是某人表达了什么观点，其中包含了两大考点：一是考查发出观点的人（作者或者其他人物）；二是考查观点的内容细节。常见的提问形式如下：

Sb. think/believe/hold/suggest that...

According to sb.,...

An argument made by sb. is that...

观点题的解题步骤是：

①确定发出观点的人：先审题干，如果考查的是作者之外的人物的观点，那么要先去原文中定位，找到发出观点的这个人；但如果考查的是作者的观点，通常作者极少在文章中直接出现，因此不需要去原文中定位，只要记得没有明确说明是谁的观点的内容都是作者的观点，因为文章就是作者写的。

②比对观点的内容细节：逐个比对选项和原文，采用静姐的“灵魂三问”法。观点题在考查观点的内容细节时，其实就是结合了细节题或推断题，因此解题的方法同细节题的“灵魂三问”。

注意：多方观点汇集处一定会出题，会提问一方的观点，用其他人的观点来作为错误的混淆项。比如下面的例25，一共出现了三方观点，这三方分别是Freud（弗洛伊德）、neurologists（神经病学家们）和Researchers（研究人员），题目问的是“研究人员的观点”，然后故意用另外两方的观点来混淆，因此就有了错误选项C（弗洛伊德的观点）和D（神经病学家们的观点）。再比如下面的例26，审题干，题目是The author believes that the devoted concertgoers（作者认为音乐会忠实听众），分清主句和从句之后，会发现题干问的是“作者的观点”，而不是“音乐会忠实听众”的观点，一定要区分清楚。

##### 例25: 2005年Text 3

①Of all the components of a good night's sleep, dreams seem to be least within our control. ②In dreams, a window opens into a world where logic is suspended and dead people speak. ③A century ago, Freud formulated his revolutionary theory that dreams were the disguised shadows of our unconscious desires and fears; by the late 1970s, neurologists had switched to thinking of them as just "mental noise" —the random byproducts of the neural-repair work that goes on during sleep. ④Now  $ \underline{\text{researchers}} $ suspect that  $ \underline{\text{dreams}} $ are part of the mind's emotional thermostat, regulating moods while the brain is "off-line." ⑤And one leading authority says that these intensely powerful mental events can be not only harnessed but actually brought under conscious control, to help us sleep and feel better. ⑥"It's your  $ \underline{\text{dream}} $," says Rosalind Cartwright, chair of psychology at Chicago's Medical Center. ⑦"If you don't like it, change it."

①在一夜好眠的所有因素中，梦似乎是最不受控制的。②在梦中，有一扇窗通向逻辑暂时失效、死去的人开口说话的世界。③一个世纪前，弗洛伊德阐述了他革命性的理论——梦是人们无意识的欲望和恐惧经伪装后的影子；到了20世纪70年代末期，神经病学家们转而认为它们（梦）仅仅是“精神噪声”——在睡眠期间进行神经修复活动的随机副产品。④现在，研究人员认为梦是大脑情绪自动调节系统的一部分，当大脑处于“离线”状态时，（梦）对情绪进行调节。⑤一位重要的权威人士说，（梦）这种异常强烈的精神活动不仅能被利用，而且事实上还可以被有意识地加以控制，以帮助我们睡得更好和感觉更舒服。⑥芝加哥医疗中心心理学系主任罗莎琳德 卡特赖特说：“这是你的梦。⑦如果你不喜欢它，那就改变它。”

###  $ \underline{\text{Researchers}} $ have come to believe that  $ \underline{\text{dreams}} $研究人员已经逐渐相信梦



<table border=1 style='margin: auto; word-wrap: break-word;'><tr><td style='text-align: center; word-wrap: break-word;'>[A]</td><td style='text-align: center; word-wrap: break-word;'>can be modified in their courses.在形成过程中可以被改变。</td><td style='text-align: center; word-wrap: break-word;'>【段1】④Now researchers suspect that dreams... ⑥“It’s your dream,” says Rosalind Cartwright, chair of psychology at Chicago’s Medical Center. ⑦“If you don’t like it, change it.”根据题干中的 Researchers 和 dreams 可以定位到段1，句④至句⑦说的都是 researchers（研究人员）的观点，因此先把谁的观点确定了。选项中的 modified（改变）对应原文中的 change（改变，变化），属于同义改写。原文说“这是你的梦。如果你不喜欢它，那就改变它”，而题干+选项说“研究人员已经逐渐相信梦在形成过程中可以被改变”，正好是对原文的同义改写，因此 A 选项正确。</td></tr><tr><td style='text-align: center; word-wrap: break-word;'>[B]</td><td style='text-align: center; word-wrap: break-word;'>are susceptible to emotional changes.容易受到情绪变化的影响。</td><td style='text-align: center; word-wrap: break-word;'>【段1】④Now researchers suspect that dreams are part of the mind’s emotional thermostat, regulating moods while the brain is “off-line.”选项中的 emotional（情绪的）在原文中可以找到，且对应原文中的 moods（情绪）。原文说的是“梦是大脑情绪自动调节系统的一部分，……（梦）对情绪进行调节”，即“梦（主动）调节情绪”；而选项说的是“梦容易受到情绪变化的影响”，即“梦被情绪影响”，选项和原文表达的内容是相反的，属于反向干扰，因此 B 选项错误。</td></tr><tr><td style='text-align: center; word-wrap: break-word;'>[C]</td><td style='text-align: center; word-wrap: break-word;'>reflect our innermost desires and fears.反映我们内心深处的欲望与恐惧。</td><td style='text-align: center; word-wrap: break-word;'>【段1】③ A century ago, Freud formulated his revolutionary theory that dreams were the disguised shadows of our unconscious desires and fears...通过选项中的关键词 desires and fears，可以定位到段1句③。这是弗洛伊德（Freud）的观点，与题干提问的“研究人员”的观点不匹配，因此都不用仔细看内容的细节，直接可以判定是错误选项。</td></tr><tr><td style='text-align: center; word-wrap: break-word;'>[D]</td><td style='text-align: center; word-wrap: break-word;'>are a random outcome of neural repairs.是神经修复中随机（产生）的结果。</td><td style='text-align: center; word-wrap: break-word;'>【段1】③...by the late 1970s, neurologists had switched to thinking of them as just “mental noise”—the random byproducts of the neural-repair work that goes on during sleep.选项中的关键词 random outcome of neural repairs [神经修复中随机（产生）的结果]，对应原文 random byproducts of the neural-repair（神经修复活动的随机副产品），属于同义改写，由此可以定位到段1句③。这是神经病学家们的观点，与题干提问的“研究人员”的观点不匹配，因此都不用仔细看内容的细节，直接可以判定是错误选项。</td></tr></table>

##### 例26：英语一2011年Text1

<div style="text-align: center;"><img src="https://pplines-online.bj.bcebos.com/deploy/official/paddleocr/pp-ocr-vl-16-online//54b730ea-3c41-4517-afe5-b2e20d6bd190/markdown_4/imgs/img_in_image_box_195_210_262_229.jpg?authorization=bce-auth-v1%2FALTAKDN8mY5KlNI7zaRpLmOqrw%2F2026-06-22T15%3A15%3A56Z%2F-1%2F%2F7508f456e6df6a3120c40d06a993dc7f43223076ccb2329d2b9db42e40a79b4c" alt="Image" width="5%" />

<div style="text-align: center;"><img src="https://pplines-online.bj.bcebos.com/deploy/official/paddleocr/pp-ocr-vl-16-online//54b730ea-3c41-4517-afe5-b2e20d6bd190/markdown_4/imgs/img_in_image_box_195_210_262_229.jpg?authorization=bce-auth-v1%2FALTAKDN8mY5KlNI7zaRpLmOqrw%2F2026-06-22T15%3A15%3A56Z%2F-1%2F%2F7508f456e6df6a3120c40d06a993dc7f43223076ccb2329d2b9db42e40a79b4c" alt="Image" width="5%" />

～

</div>


</div>


① $ \underline{\text{Devoted concertgoers}} $ who reply that recordings are no substitute for live performance are missing the point. ②For the time, attention, and money of the art-loving public, classical instrumentalists must compete not only with opera houses, dance troupes, theater companies, and museums, but also with the recorded performances of the great classical musicians of the 20th century. ③These recordings are cheap, available everywhere, and very often much higher in artistic quality than today's live performances; moreover, they can be "consumed" at a time and place of the listener s choosing. ④The widespread availability of such recordings has thus brought about a crisis in the institution of the traditional classical concert.

①回应为“音乐录制品绝不会取代现场演奏”的音乐会忠实听众没有抓住要点。②为了（获得）艺术爱好者的时间、关注和金钱，古典乐器演奏家们不仅必须和歌剧院、舞蹈团、剧团以及博物馆竞争，而且还必须和20世纪伟大的古典音乐家的演奏录制品竞争。③这些录制品价格低廉，随处可得，而且其艺术品质往往比当今现场音乐会的更高，再者，它们可以在听众选择的（任何）时间、（任何）地点被“消费”。④这些音乐录制品的广泛可得（的性质）给（听）传统古典音乐会的习俗带来了危机。

### 23 The author believes that the  $ \underline{\text{devoted concertgoers}} $作者认为音乐会忠实听众



<table border=1 style='margin: auto; word-wrap: break-word;'><tr><td colspan="3">题干定位 根据题干中的关键词 devoted concertgoers 可以定位到段4。</td></tr><tr><td style='text-align: center; word-wrap: break-word;'>[A] ignore the expenses  $ \underline{\text{of}} $  $ \underline{\text{live performances}} $. 忽视现场演奏的开销。</td><td rowspan="2" colspan="2">【段4】① Devoted concertgoers who reply that recordings are no substitute for  $ \underline{\text{live performance}} $ are missing the point. ③ These recordings are cheap, available everywhere, and very often much higher in artistic quality than today&#x27;s  $ \underline{\text{live performances}} $... ④ The widespread availability of such recordings has thus brought about a crisis in the institution of the traditional classical concert. A、C、D选项中均包含关键词live performances（现场演奏），可以结合在一起看。原文段4句①提到音乐会忠实听众认为“音乐录制品绝不会取代现场演奏”，但作者认为他们没有抓住要点，句③~④中，作者列出音乐录制品相比于现场演奏的各种优点——价格低廉、随时随地都能听、广泛可得，由此可知，作者认为现场演奏并没有那么好，音乐会忠实听众高估了现场演奏的价值，D选项是对原文段4句①和句③~④内容的高度概括，因此D选项正确。其他三个选项的分析如下：A选项中的“忽视开销”和C选项中的“夸大种类”均未在原文提及，属于捏造信息，因此都错误。</td></tr><tr><td style='text-align: center; word-wrap: break-word;'>[B] reject most kinds of  $ \underline{\text{recorded performances}} $. 排斥大多数种类的演奏录制。</td><td style='text-align: center; word-wrap: break-word;'></td></tr></table>
